(**********************************************************************************

 Squares in a 2-category

 We define the 2-sided displayed category of squares in a 2-category. Here we require
 the squares to be given by 2-cells rather than equalities.

 In general this construction does not give rise to a univalent 2-sided displayed
 category even when we assume that the 2-category to be univalent. The reason for that
 the univalence of this 2-sided displayed category requires local univalence from the
 2-category. While this condition is not necessarily satisfied by univalent 2-categories,
 it is satisfied by, for example, categories enriched over posets.

 Contents
 1. Definition via two-sided displayed categories
 2. Univalence and strictness

 **********************************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

C: two_cat
C → C → UU
 exact (λ x y, x --> y).
    
C: two_cat
(λ D : C → C → UU,
 ∏ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ : C,
 D x₁ y₁ → D x₂ y₂ → C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧ → C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧ → UU)
  (λ x y : C, C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
 exact (λ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ h₁ h₂ f g, h₁ · g ==> f · h₂).
  Defined.

C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
xy₃: pr11 C ⟦ x₃, y₃ ⟧
f₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
g₁: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: pr11 C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
τ: xy₁ · g₁ ==> f₁ · xy₂
θ: xy₂ · g₂ ==> f₂ · xy₃
xy₁ · (g₁ · g₂) ==> f₁ · f₂ · xy₃

      exact (two_cat_lassociator _ _ _
             • (τ ▹ _)
             • two_cat_rassociator _ _ _
             • (_ ◃ θ)
             • two_cat_lassociator _ _ _).
  Defined.

C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
f, f': C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
p: f' = f
g, g': C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
q: g' = g
h₁: two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
h₂: two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
τ: h₁ -->[ f ][ g] h₂
trb₂ τ =
((h₁ ◃ idto2mor q) • τ) • (idto2mor (! p) ▹ h₂)

C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
f': C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g': C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
h₁: two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat_data x₁ y₁
h₂: two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
τ: h₁ -->[ f' ][ g'] h₂
trb₂ τ =
((h₁ ◃ idto2mor (idpath g')) • τ)
• (idto2mor (! idpath f') ▹ h₂)

    
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C

τ: h₁ -->[ f' ][ g'] h₂
τ = ((h₁ ◃ id2 g') • τ) • (id2 f' ▹ h₂)

    
C: two_cat

τ: h₁ -->[ f' ][ g'] h₂
τ = (id2 (h₁ · g') • τ) • (id2 f' ▹ h₂)

    
C: two_cat

τ: h₁ -->[ f' ][ g'] h₂
τ = (id2 (h₁ · g') • τ) • id2 (f' · h₂)

    
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C

h₂: two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat_data x₂ y₂
τ: h₁ -->[ f' ][ g'] h₂
τ = τ • id2 (f' · h₂)

  Qed.

C: two_cat
id_two_disp_left_law
  two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat_data
 
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
f: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ · g ==> f · xy₂
(((two_cat_lassociator xy₁ (identity y₁) g
   • ((two_cat_runitor xy₁ • two_cat_linvunitor xy₁)
      ▹ g)) • two_cat_rassociator (identity x₁) xy₁ g)
 • (identity x₁ ◃ fg))
• two_cat_lassociator (identity x₁) f xy₂ = trb₂ fg

      
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
f: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ · g ==> f · xy₂
(((two_cat_lassociator xy₁ (identity y₁) g
   • ((two_cat_runitor xy₁ • two_cat_linvunitor xy₁)
      ▹ g)) • two_cat_rassociator (identity x₁) xy₁ g)
 • (identity x₁ ◃ fg))
• two_cat_lassociator (identity x₁) f xy₂ =
((xy₁ ◃ idto2mor (id_left g)) • fg)
• (idto2mor (! id_left f) ▹ xy₂)

      
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
f: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ · g ==> f · xy₂
(((idto2mor (assoc xy₁ (identity y₁) g)
   • ((idto2mor (id_right xy₁)
       • idto2mor (! id_left xy₁)) ▹ g))
  • idto2mor (! assoc (identity x₁) xy₁ g))
 • (identity x₁ ◃ fg))
• idto2mor (assoc (identity x₁) f xy₂) =
((xy₁ ◃ idto2mor (id_left g)) • fg)
• (idto2mor (! id_left f) ▹ xy₂)

      
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
f: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ · g ==> f · xy₂
(((idto2mor (assoc xy₁ (identity y₁) g)
   • ((idto2mor (id_right xy₁)
       • idto2mor (! id_left xy₁)) ▹ g))
  • idto2mor (! assoc (identity x₁) xy₁ g))
 • (identity x₁ ◃ fg))
• idto2mor (assoc (identity x₁) f xy₂) =
(idto2mor
   (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, xy₁ · q)
      (id_left g)) • fg)
• (idto2mor (! id_left f) ▹ xy₂)

      
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
f: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ · g ==> f · xy₂
(((idto2mor (assoc xy₁ (identity y₁) g)
   • ((idto2mor (id_right xy₁)
       • idto2mor (! id_left xy₁)) ▹ g))
  • idto2mor (! assoc (identity x₁) xy₁ g))
 • (identity x₁ ◃ fg))
• idto2mor (assoc (identity x₁) f xy₂) =
(idto2mor
   (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, xy₁ · q)
      (id_left g)) • fg)
• idto2mor
    (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧, q · xy₂)
       (! id_left f))

      
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
f: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ · g ==> f · xy₂
(((idto2mor (assoc xy₁ (identity y₁) g)
   • (idto2mor (id_right xy₁ @ ! id_left xy₁) ▹ g))
  • idto2mor (! assoc (identity x₁) xy₁ g))
 • (identity x₁ ◃ fg))
• idto2mor (assoc (identity x₁) f xy₂) =
(idto2mor
   (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, xy₁ · q)
      (id_left g)) • fg)
• idto2mor
    (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧, q · xy₂)
       (! id_left f))

      
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
f: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ · g ==> f · xy₂
(((idto2mor (assoc xy₁ (identity y₁) g)
   • idto2mor
       (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧, q · g)
          (id_right xy₁ @ ! id_left xy₁)))
  • idto2mor (! assoc (identity x₁) xy₁ g))
 • (identity x₁ ◃ fg))
• idto2mor (assoc (identity x₁) f xy₂) =
(idto2mor
   (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, xy₁ · q)
      (id_left g)) • fg)
• idto2mor
    (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧, q · xy₂)
       (! id_left f))

      
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
f: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg: xy₁ · g ==> f · xy₂
(idto2mor
   ((assoc xy₁ (identity y₁) g @
     maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧, q · g)
       (id_right xy₁ @ ! id_left xy₁)) @
    ! assoc (identity x₁) xy₁ g) • (identity x₁ ◃ fg))
• idto2mor (assoc (identity x₁) f xy₂) =
(idto2mor
   (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧, xy₁ · q)
      (id_left g)) • fg)
• idto2mor
    (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧, q · xy₂)
       (! id_left f))

       (id_right xy₁ @ ! id_left xy₁)) @
    ! assoc (identity x₁) xy₁ g) • (identity x₁ ◃ fg))
• idto2mor (assoc (identity x₁) f xy₂) = ?b

C: two_cat

f₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: pr11 C ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧
g₁: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: pr11 C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: pr11 C ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ · g₁ ==> f₁ · xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ · g₂ ==> f₂ · xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ · g₃ ==> f₃ · xy₄
(((two_cat_lassociator xy₁ g₁ (g₂ · g₃)
   • (fg₁ ▹ g₂ · g₃))
  • two_cat_rassociator f₁ xy₂ (g₂ · g₃))
 • (f₁
    ◃ ((((two_cat_lassociator xy₂ g₂ g₃ • (fg₂ ▹ g₃))
         • two_cat_rassociator f₂ xy₃ g₃) • (f₂ ◃ fg₃))
       • two_cat_lassociator f₂ f₃ xy₄)))
• two_cat_lassociator f₁ (f₂ · f₃) xy₄ =
trb₂ ((((two_cat_lassociator xy₁ (g₁ · g₂) g₃
         • (((((two_cat_lassociator xy₁ g₁ g₂
                • (fg₁ ▹ g₂))
               • two_cat_rassociator f₁ xy₂ g₂)
              • (f₁ ◃ fg₂))
             • two_cat_lassociator f₁ f₂ xy₃) ▹ g₃))
        • two_cat_rassociator (f₁ · f₂) xy₃ g₃)
       • (f₁ · f₂ ◃ fg₃))
      • two_cat_lassociator (f₁ · f₂) f₃ xy₄)

        (assoc f₂ f₃ xy₄)))

    (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧, q · xy₄)
       (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃))

                      (maponpaths

                       assoc f₁ (f₂ · f₃) xy₄))))))) =

  ((maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧, xy₁ · q)

g₁: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: pr11 C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: pr11 C ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ · g₁ ==> f₁ · xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ · g₂ ==> f₂ · xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ · g₃ ==> f₃ · xy₄
idto2mor (assoc xy₁ g₁ (g₂ · g₃))
• (((idto2mor (assoc (xy₁ · g₁) g₂ g₃)
     • ((fg₁ ▹ g₂) ▹ g₃))
    • idto2mor (! assoc (f₁ · xy₂) g₂ g₃))
   • (idto2mor (! assoc f₁ xy₂ (g₂ · g₃))
      • (idto2mor
           (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
              (assoc xy₂ g₂ g₃))
         • ((f₁ ◃ (fg₂ ▹ g₃))
            • (idto2mor
                 (maponpaths
                    (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
                    (! assoc f₂ xy₃ g₃))
               • ((f₁ ◃ (f₂ ◃ fg₃))
                  • idto2mor
                      (maponpaths
                         (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
                         (assoc f₂ f₃ xy₄) @
                       assoc f₁ (f₂ · f₃) xy₄))))))) =
idto2mor
  ((maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧, xy₁ · q)
      (assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) @ assoc xy₁ (g₁ · g₂) g₃) @
   maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
     (assoc xy₁ g₁ g₂))
• (((fg₁ ▹ g₂) ▹ g₃)
   • (idto2mor
        (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
           (! assoc f₁ xy₂ g₂))
      • (((f₁ ◃ fg₂) ▹ g₃)
         • (idto2mor
              (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
                 (assoc f₁ f₂ xy₃))
            • (idto2mor (! assoc (f₁ · f₂) xy₃ g₃)
               • ((f₁ · f₂ ◃ fg₃)
                  • idto2mor
                      (assoc (f₁ · f₂) f₃ xy₄ @
                       maponpaths
                         (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧, q · xy₄)
                         (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃))))))))

      
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄, y₁, y₂, y₃, y₄: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
xy₃: pr11 C ⟦ x₃, y₃ ⟧
xy₄: pr11 C ⟦ x₄, y₄ ⟧
f₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: pr11 C ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧
g₁: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: pr11 C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: pr11 C ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ · g₁ ==> f₁ · xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ · g₂ ==> f₂ · xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ · g₃ ==> f₃ · xy₄
((((((((idto2mor (assoc xy₁ g₁ (g₂ · g₃))
        • idto2mor (assoc (xy₁ · g₁) g₂ g₃))
       • ((fg₁ ▹ g₂) ▹ g₃))
      • idto2mor (! assoc (f₁ · xy₂) g₂ g₃))
     • idto2mor (! assoc f₁ xy₂ (g₂ · g₃)))
    • idto2mor
        (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
           (assoc xy₂ g₂ g₃))) • (f₁ ◃ (fg₂ ▹ g₃)))
  • idto2mor
      (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
         (! assoc f₂ xy₃ g₃))) • (f₁ ◃ (f₂ ◃ fg₃)))
• idto2mor
    (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
       (assoc f₂ f₃ xy₄) @ assoc f₁ (f₂ · f₃) xy₄) =
((((((idto2mor
        ((maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧, xy₁ · q)
            (assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) @ assoc xy₁ (g₁ · g₂) g₃) @
         maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
           (assoc xy₁ g₁ g₂)) • ((fg₁ ▹ g₂) ▹ g₃))
     • idto2mor
         (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
            (! assoc f₁ xy₂ g₂))) • ((f₁ ◃ fg₂) ▹ g₃))
   • idto2mor
       (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
          (assoc f₁ f₂ xy₃)))
  • idto2mor (! assoc (f₁ · f₂) xy₃ g₃))
 • (f₁ · f₂ ◃ fg₃))
• idto2mor
    (assoc (f₁ · f₂) f₃ xy₄ @
     maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧, q · xy₄)
       (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃))

       ! assoc f₁ xy₂ (g₂ · g₃)) @

C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄, y₁, y₂, y₃, y₄: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
xy₃: pr11 C ⟦ x₃, y₃ ⟧
xy₄: pr11 C ⟦ x₄, y₄ ⟧
f₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: pr11 C ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧
g₁: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: pr11 C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: pr11 C ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ · g₁ ==> f₁ · xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ · g₂ ==> f₂ · xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ · g₃ ==> f₃ · xy₄
idto2mor
  (assoc xy₁ g₁ (g₂ · g₃) @ assoc (xy₁ · g₁) g₂ g₃)
• (((fg₁ ▹ g₂) ▹ g₃)
   • (idto2mor
        (((! assoc (f₁ · xy₂) g₂ g₃ @
           ! assoc f₁ xy₂ (g₂ · g₃)) @
          maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
            (assoc xy₂ g₂ g₃)) @
         assoc f₁ (xy₂ · g₂) g₃)
      • (((f₁ ◃ fg₂) ▹ g₃)
         • (idto2mor
              ((! assoc f₁ (f₂ · xy₃) g₃ @
                maponpaths
                  (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
                  (! assoc f₂ xy₃ g₃)) @
               assoc f₁ f₂ (xy₃ · g₃))
            • ((f₁ · f₂ ◃ fg₃)
               • idto2mor
                   (! assoc f₁ f₂ (f₃ · xy₄) @
                    maponpaths
                      (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
                      (assoc f₂ f₃ xy₄) @
                    assoc f₁ (f₂ · f₃) xy₄)))))) =
idto2mor
  ((maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧, xy₁ · q)
      (assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) @ assoc xy₁ (g₁ · g₂) g₃) @
   maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
     (assoc xy₁ g₁ g₂))
• (((fg₁ ▹ g₂) ▹ g₃)
   • (idto2mor
        (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
           (! assoc f₁ xy₂ g₂))
      • (((f₁ ◃ fg₂) ▹ g₃)
         • (idto2mor
              (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
                 (assoc f₁ f₂ xy₃))
            • (idto2mor (! assoc (f₁ · f₂) xy₃ g₃)
               • ((f₁ · f₂ ◃ fg₃)
                  • idto2mor
                      (assoc (f₁ · f₂) f₃ xy₄ @
                       maponpaths
                         (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧, q · xy₄)
                         (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃))))))))

      
C: two_cat
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄, y₁, y₂, y₃, y₄: pr11 C
xy₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
xy₃: pr11 C ⟦ x₃, y₃ ⟧
xy₄: pr11 C ⟦ x₄, y₄ ⟧
f₁: pr11 C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: pr11 C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
f₃: pr11 C ⟦ x₃, x₄ ⟧
g₁: pr11 C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂: pr11 C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
g₃: pr11 C ⟦ y₃, y₄ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ · g₁ ==> f₁ · xy₂
fg₂: xy₂ · g₂ ==> f₂ · xy₃
fg₃: xy₃ · g₃ ==> f₃ · xy₄
idto2mor
  ((maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y₁, y₄ ⟧, xy₁ · q)
      (assoc g₁ g₂ g₃) @ assoc xy₁ (g₁ · g₂) g₃) @
   maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
     (assoc xy₁ g₁ g₂))
• (((fg₁ ▹ g₂) ▹ g₃)
   • (idto2mor
        (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
           (! assoc f₁ xy₂ g₂))
      • (((f₁ ◃ fg₂) ▹ g₃)
         • (idto2mor
              (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, y₃ ⟧, q · g₃)
                 (assoc f₁ f₂ xy₃))
            • (idto2mor (! assoc (f₁ · f₂) xy₃ g₃)
               • ((f₁ · f₂ ◃ fg₃)
                  • idto2mor
                      (assoc (f₁ · f₂) f₃ xy₄ @
                       maponpaths
                         (λ q : C ⟦ x₁, x₄ ⟧, q · xy₄)
                         (! assoc f₁ f₂ f₃)))))))) =
idto2mor
  (assoc xy₁ g₁ (g₂ · g₃) @ assoc (xy₁ · g₁) g₂ g₃)
• (((fg₁ ▹ g₂) ▹ g₃)
   • (idto2mor
        (((! assoc (f₁ · xy₂) g₂ g₃ @
           ! assoc f₁ xy₂ (g₂ · g₃)) @
          maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
            (assoc xy₂ g₂ g₃)) @
         assoc f₁ (xy₂ · g₂) g₃)
      • (((f₁ ◃ fg₂) ▹ g₃)
         • (idto2mor
              ((! assoc f₁ (f₂ · xy₃) g₃ @
                maponpaths
                  (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
                  (! assoc f₂ xy₃ g₃)) @
               assoc f₁ f₂ (xy₃ · g₃))
            • ((f₁ · f₂ ◃ fg₃)
               • idto2mor
                   (! assoc f₁ f₂ (f₃ · xy₄) @
                    maponpaths
                      (λ q : C ⟦ x₂, y₄ ⟧, f₁ · q)
                      (assoc f₂ f₃ xy₄) @
                    assoc f₁ (f₂ · f₃) xy₄))))))

  Section IsoToDisp.
    Context {x y : C}
            {f g : two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat x y}
            (τ : z_iso (C := hom_cat x y) f g).

    Let θ : f -->[ identity x ][ identity y ] g
      := two_cat_runitor _ • pr1 τ • two_cat_linvunitor _.

    Let θi : g -->[ identity x ][ identity y ] f
      := two_cat_runitor _ • inv_from_z_iso τ • two_cat_linvunitor _.

    
C: two_cat
x, y: C
f, g: two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat x y
τ: z_iso f g
θ:= (two_cat_runitor f • pr1 τ) • two_cat_linvunitor g: f -->[ identity x ][ identity y] g
θi:= (two_cat_runitor g • inv_from_z_iso τ)
• two_cat_linvunitor f: g -->[ identity x ][ identity y] f
θ ;;2 θi = trb₂ id_two_disp f

 • two_cat_linvunitor f) = trb₂ id_two_disp f

       • two_cat_linvunitor g) ▹ identity y))
  • two_cat_rassociator (identity x) g (identity y))
 • (identity x
    ◃ ((two_cat_runitor g • inv_from_z_iso τ)
       • two_cat_linvunitor f)))
• two_cat_lassociator (identity x) (identity x) f =
((f ◃ idto2mor (id_left (identity y)))
 • (two_cat_runitor f • two_cat_linvunitor f))
• (idto2mor (! id_left (identity x)) ▹ f)

  Section DispToIso.
    Context {x y : C}
            {f g : two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat x y}
            (τ : iso_twosided_disp (identity_z_iso x) (identity_z_iso y) f g).

      := two_cat_rinvunitor _ • pr1 τ • two_cat_lunitor _.

    Let θi : g ==> f
      := two_cat_rinvunitor _ • iso_inv_twosided_disp τ • two_cat_lunitor _.

  (identity_z_iso y) f g
θ:= (two_cat_rinvunitor f • pr1 τ) • two_cat_lunitor g: f ==> g
θi:= (two_cat_rinvunitor g • iso_inv_twosided_disp τ)
• two_cat_lunitor f: g ==> f
p: (((two_cat_lassociator f (identity y) (identity y)
   • (τ ▹ identity y))
  • two_cat_rassociator (identity x) g
      (identity y))
 • (identity x ◃ iso_inv_twosided_disp τ))
• two_cat_lassociator (identity x) (identity x) f =
(idto2mor
   (maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y, y ⟧, f · q)
      (id_left (identity y)))
 • (idto2mor (id_right f) • idto2mor (! id_left f)))
• (idto2mor (! id_left (identity x)) ▹ f)
((idto2mor (! id_right f) • pr1 τ)
 • idto2mor (id_left g))
• ((idto2mor (! id_right g) • iso_inv_twosided_disp τ)
   • idto2mor (id_left f)) = id2 f

   • (idto2mor (id_left g)

     ((maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ y, y ⟧, g · q)
         (id_left (identity y)) @
       id_right g @ ! id_left g) @
      maponpaths (λ q : C ⟦ x, x ⟧, q · g)
        (! id_left (identity x)))) • idto2mor q₂ =

x, y: C

transportf
  (λ z : C, two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat z y)
  (idpath x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C, two_cat_arrow_twosided_disp_cat x z)
     (idpath y) f) = g
≃ iso_twosided_disp (idtoiso (idpath x))
    (idtoiso (idpath y)) f g
